pipeline in C++. Here are the key components:\\n\\n### 1. Abstract CertValidator Interface\\nThe abstract interface `CertValidator` (source/common/tls/cert_validator/cert_validator.h) defines the contract for certificate validators. It includes pure virtual methods:\\n- `addClientValidationContext()`: Adds client validation context to SSL_CTX\\n- `doVerifyCertChain()`: Performs certificate chain verification (synchronous or asynchronous)\\n- `initializeSslContexts()`: Initializes SSL contexts for validation\\n- `updateDigestForSessionId()`: Updates digest for session ID generation\\n- `getCaCertInformation()`: Returns CA certificate details\\n\\n### 2. DefaultCertValidator with X.509 Chain Verification\\nThe `DefaultCertValidator` class (source/common/tls/cert_validator/default_validator.h and .cc) implements standard X.509 certificate chain verification. Key features:\\n- Loads trusted CA certificates from PEM files\\n- Performs X.509 chain verification using BoringSSL\\n- Supports certificate pinning via:\\n  - `verifyCertificateHashList()`: SHA-256 DER-encoded certificate hash pinning\\n  - `verifyCertificateSpkiList()`: Base64-encoded SPKI hash pinning\\n- Validates Subject Alternative Names through `verifySubjectAltName()` and `matchSubjectAltName()`\\n- Handles untrusted certificate policies\\n\\n### 3. SAN Matcher for Subject Alternative Name Matching\\nThe `SanMatcher` interface and `StringSanMatcher` implementation (source/common/tls/cert_validator/san_matcher.h and .cc) handle Subject Alternative Name matching for:\\n- **DNS names** (GEN_DNS): With proper DNS name matching semantics\\n- **URIs** (GEN_URI): For URI-based SANs\\n- **Email addresses** (GEN_EMAIL): For email-based SANs\\n- **IP addresses** (GEN_IPADD): For IP-based SANs\\n- **Other names** (GEN_OTHERNAME): Custom OID-based SANs\\n\\nThe `createStringSanMatcher()` factory function creates appropriate matchers based on configuration.\\n\\n### 4. ContextImpl Managing TLS Certificates and OCSP\\nThe `ContextImpl` class (source/common/tls/context_impl.h and .cc) is the base class that:\\n- Manages a vector of `TlsContext` structures containing:\\n  - SSL_CTX pointers\\n  - X.509 certificate chains\\n  - `OcspResponseWrapper` for OCSP stapling\\n  - Private key information\\n- Implements custom certificate verification via `customVerifyCallback()` and `customVerifyCertChain()`\\n- Delegates actual validation to the `CertValidator` instance\\n- Provides asynchronous certificate validation through callback mechanisms\\n\\n### 5. ServerContextImpl with OCSP Stapling\\nThe `ServerContextImpl` class (source/common/tls/server_context_impl.h and .cc) extends ContextImpl with:\\n- OCSP stapling support through `ocspStapleAction()` and `findTlsContext()`\\n- `OcspStapleAction` enum for controlling OCSP response stapling (Staple, NoStaple, Fail, ClientNotCapable)\\n- Certificate selection based on SNI and client capabilities\\n- Management of server-side contexts and session tickets\\n\\n### 6. OCSP Response Parsing and Stapling Support\\n\\n#### OcspResponse and Related Structures (source/common/tls/ocsp/ocsp.h and .cc)\\nKey types and classes:\\n- **OcspResponseStatus**: Enumeration for OCSP response status (Successful, MalformedRequest, InternalError, TryLater, SigRequired, Unauthorized)\\n- **CertId**: Structure containing certificate serial number for OCSP identification\\n- **SingleResponse**: Contains cert status and validity period (thisUpdate, nextUpdate)\\n- **ResponseData**: Collection of SingleResponse elements\\n- **BasicOcspResponse**: Implements the RFC 6960 BasicOcspResponse format\\n- **OcspResponseWrapperImpl**: Wraps OCSP responses and provides:\\n  - `matchesCertificate()`: Verifies OCSP response matches a certificate\\n  - `secondsUntilExpiration()`: Calculates response validity\\n  - `isExpired()`: Checks if response is expired\\n  - `rawBytes()`: Returns DER-encoded response for stapling\\n\\n#### ASN.1 Parsing Utilities (source/common/tls/ocsp/asn1_utility.h and .cc)\\nThe `Asn1Utility` class provides template-based ASN.1 DER parsing:\\n- `parseOid()`: Parses OBJECT IDENTIFIER elements\\n- `parseGeneralizedTime()`: Parses GENERALIZEDTIME elements (UTC format enforced)\\n- `parseInteger()`: Parses arbitrary-precision INTEGER elements\\n- `parseOctetString()`: Parses OCTET STRING elements\\n- `parseSequenceOf()`: Template for parsing SEQUENCE OF structures\\n- `parseOptional()`: Template for parsing explicitly tagged optional elements\\n\\nThe `Asn1OcspUtility` class provides OCSP-specific parsing:\\n- `parseOcspResponse()`: Parses top-level OCSP response\\n- `parseResponseStatus()`: Extracts response status\\n- `parseResponseBytes()`: Parses response bytes with OID matching for BasicOcspResponse\\n- `parseBasicOcspResponse()`: Parses BasicOcspResponse structure\\n- `parseResponseData()`: Extracts response validity period and certificate statuses\\n- `parseSingleResponse()`: Parses individual certificate status\\n- `parseCertId()`: Extracts certificate identification information\\n\\n### 7. ClientContextImpl\\nThe `ClientContextImpl` class (source/common/tls/client_context_impl.h and .cc) extends ContextImpl for client-side TLS with:\\n- Server Name Indication (SNI) support\\n- Session reuse management\\n- Client certificate configuration validation\\n- Renegotiation control\\n\\n### 8. SPIFFE Validator Extension\\nThe `SPIFFEValidator` class (source/extensions/transport_sockets/tls/cert_validator/spiffe/spiffe_validator.h and .cc) implements SPIFFE-specific certificate validation:\\n- Extends the `CertValidator` interface\\n- Extracts SPIFFE trust domain from certificate SANs\\n- Maintains per-trust-domain X509_STORE instances\\n- Validates certificates against trust domain-specific CA bundles\\n- Supports certificate expiration flexibility\\n\\n### 9. Certificate Validation Factory\\nThe `CertValidatorFactory` interface (source/common/tls/cert_validator/factory.h and .cc) provides:\\n- Factory registration mechanism for different validator implementations\\n- `createCertValidator()`: Creates appropriate validator instances\\n- Support for both default and custom validators like SPIFFEValidator\\n\\n### Validation Flow\\nThe complete TLS certificate validation pipeline works as follows:\\n1. ContextImpl receives SSL handshake events\\n2. customVerifyCallback is invoked by OpenSSL\\n3. Certificate chain is passed to CertValidator::doVerifyCertChain()\\n4. DefaultCertValidator (or custom validator) performs:\\n   - X.509 chain verification against trusted CAs\\n   - Subject Alternative Name matching using SanMatcher\\n   - Certificate pinning checks\\n   - Certificate expiration validation\\n5. For OCSP stapling (server-side):\\n   - Server finds appropriate TlsContext\\n   - Determines if OCSP response should be stapled\\n   - OCSP response is parsed and verified using Asn1OcspUtility\\n   - Response is included in ServerHello if stapling is enabled\\n6. Validation results are returned to SSL layer\\n7. Asynchronous validations use callbacks for deferred processing\\n\\nAll certificate validation is backed by BoringSSL, which provides FIPS-capable cryptographic operations for X.509 processing.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1581,"cache_read_input_tokens":57310,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1581},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"6b9665aa-ae4e-4985-8118-7c4f129e5cc8","uuid":"125aecae-fa3b-43a4-9f94-62fb61a995f3"}

It includes pure virtual methods:\\n- `addClientValidationContext()`: Adds client validation context to SSL_CTX\\n- `doVerifyCertChain()`: Performs certificate chain verification (synchronous or asynchronous)\\n- `initializeSslContexts()`: Initializes SSL contexts for validation\\n- `updateDigestForSessionId()`: Updates digest for session ID generation\\n- `getCaCertInformation()`: Returns CA certificate details\\n\\n### 2. DefaultCertValidator with X.509 Chain Verification\\nThe `DefaultCertValidator` class (source/common/tls/cert_validator/default_validator.h and .cc) implements standard X.509 certificate chain verification. Key features:\\n- Loads trusted CA certificates from PEM files\\n- Performs X.509 chain verification using BoringSSL\\n- Supports certificate pinning via:\\n  - `verifyCertificateHashList()`: SHA-256 DER-encoded certificate hash pinning\\n  - `verifyCertificateSpkiList()`: Base64-encoded SPKI hash pinning\\n- Validates Subject Alternative Names through `verifySubjectAltName()` and `matchSubjectAltName()`\\n- Handles untrusted certificate policies\\n\\n### 3. SAN Matcher for Subject Alternative Name Matching\\nThe `SanMatcher` interface and `StringSanMatcher` implementation (source/common/tls/cert_validator/san_matcher.h and .cc) handle Subject Alternative Name matching for:\\n- **DNS names** (GEN_DNS): With proper DNS name matching semantics\\n- **URIs** (GEN_URI): For URI-based SANs\\n- **Email addresses** (GEN_EMAIL): For email-based SANs\\n- **IP addresses** (GEN_IPADD): For IP-based SANs\\n- **Other names** (GEN_OTHERNAME): Custom OID-based SANs\\n\\nThe `createStringSanMatcher()` factory function creates appropriate matchers based on configuration.\\n\\n### 4. ContextImpl Managing TLS Certificates and OCSP\\nThe `ContextImpl` class (source/common/tls/context_impl.h and .cc) is the base class that:\\n- Manages a vector of `TlsContext` structures containing:\\n  - SSL_CTX pointers\\n  - X.509 certificate chains\\n  - `OcspResponseWrapper` for OCSP stapling\\n  - Private key information\\n- Implements custom certificate verification via `customVerifyCallback()` and `customVerifyCertChain()`\\n- Delegates actual validation to the `CertValidator` instance\\n- Provides asynchronous certificate validation through callback mechanisms\\n\\n### 5. ServerContextImpl with OCSP Stapling\\nThe `ServerContextImpl` class (source/common/tls/server_context_impl.h and .cc) extends ContextImpl with:\\n- OCSP stapling support through `ocspStapleAction()` and `findTlsContext()`\\n- `OcspStapleAction` enum for controlling OCSP response stapling (Staple, NoStaple, Fail, ClientNotCapable)\\n- Certificate selection based on SNI and client capabilities\\n- Management of server-side contexts and session tickets\\n\\n### 6. OCSP Response Parsing and Stapling Support\\n\\n#### OcspResponse and Related Structures (source/common/tls/ocsp/ocsp.h and .cc)\\nKey types and classes:\\n- **OcspResponseStatus**: Enumeration for OCSP response status (Successful, MalformedRequest, InternalError, TryLater, SigRequired, Unauthorized)\\n- **CertId**: Structure containing certificate serial number for OCSP identification\\n- **SingleResponse**: Contains cert status and validity period (thisUpdate, nextUpdate)\\n- **ResponseData**: Collection of SingleResponse elements\\n- **BasicOcspResponse**: Implements the RFC 6960 BasicOcspResponse format\\n- **OcspResponseWrapperImpl**: Wraps OCSP responses and provides:\\n  - `matchesCertificate()`: Verifies OCSP response matches a certificate\\n  - `secondsUntilExpiration()`: Calculates response validity\\n  - `isExpired()`: Checks if response is expired\\n  - `rawBytes()`: Returns DER-encoded response for stapling\\n\\n#### ASN.1 Parsing Utilities (source/common/tls/ocsp/asn1_utility.h and .cc)\\nThe `Asn1Utility` class provides template-based ASN.1 DER parsing:\\n- `parseOid()`: Parses OBJECT IDENTIFIER elements\\n- `parseGeneralizedTime()`: Parses GENERALIZEDTIME elements (UTC format enforced)\\n- `parseInteger()`: Parses arbitrary-precision INTEGER elements\\n- `parseOctetString()`: Parses OCTET STRING elements\\n- `parseSequenceOf()`: Template for parsing SEQUENCE OF structures\\n- `parseOptional()`: Template for parsing explicitly tagged optional elements\\n\\nThe `Asn1OcspUtility` class provides OCSP-specific parsing:\\n- `parseOcspResponse()`: Parses top-level OCSP response\\n- `parseResponseStatus()`: Extracts response status\\n- `parseResponseBytes()`: Parses response bytes with OID matching for BasicOcspResponse\\n- `parseBasicOcspResponse()`: Parses BasicOcspResponse structure\\n- `parseResponseData()`: Extracts response validity period and certificate statuses\\n- `parseSingleResponse()`: Parses individual certificate status\\n- `parseCertId()`: Extracts certificate identification information\\n\\n### 7. ClientContextImpl\\nThe `ClientContextImpl` class (source/common/tls/client_context_impl.h and .cc) extends ContextImpl for client-side TLS with:\\n- Server Name Indication (SNI) support\\n- Session reuse management\\n- Client certificate configuration validation\\n- Renegotiation control\\n\\n### 8. SPIFFE Validator Extension\\nThe `SPIFFEValidator` class (source/extensions/transport_sockets/tls/cert_validator/spiffe/spiffe_validator.h and .cc) implements SPIFFE-specific certificate validation:\\n- Extends the `CertValidator` interface\\n- Extracts SPIFFE trust domain from certificate SANs\\n- Maintains per-trust-domain X509_STORE instances\\n- Validates certificates against trust domain-specific CA bundles\\n- Supports certificate expiration flexibility\\n\\n### 9. Certificate Validation Factory\\nThe `CertValidatorFactory` interface (source/common/tls/cert_validator/factory.h and .cc) provides:\\n- Factory registration mechanism for different validator implementations\\n- `createCertValidator()`: Creates appropriate validator instances\\n- Support for both default and custom validators like SPIFFEValidator\\n\\n### Validation Flow\\nThe complete TLS certificate validation pipeline works as follows:\\n1. ContextImpl receives SSL handshake events\\n2. customVerifyCallback is invoked by OpenSSL\\n3. Certificate chain is passed to CertValidator::doVerifyCertChain()\\n4. DefaultCertValidator (or custom validator) performs:\\n   - X.509 chain verification against trusted CAs\\n   - Subject Alternative Name matching using SanMatcher\\n   - Certificate pinning checks\\n   - Certificate expiration validation\\n5. For OCSP stapling (server-side):\\n   - Server finds appropriate TlsContext\\n   - Determines if OCSP response should be stapled\\n   - OCSP response is parsed and verified using Asn1OcspUtility\\n   - Response is included in ServerHello if stapling is enabled\\n6. Validation results are returned to SSL layer\\n7. Asynchronous validations use callbacks for deferred processing\\n\\nAll certificate validation is backed by BoringSSL, which provides FIPS-capable cryptographic operations for X.509 processing.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
